#BESKIDZKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA

CARPAT_01_GORCE = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = SCZ
			original_tag = LEM
			original_tag = GUR
			original_tag = BSK
		}
	}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = GUR
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2027.10.11
		ZGR = { exists = yes }			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = SCZ
					original_tag = LEM
					original_tag = BSK
				}
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2029.02.11
		ZGR = { exists = yes }	
		ZGR = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }			
		}
	}

	targets = {
		ZGR
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			original_tag = ZGR
		}
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision GAL_01_SALT_HYPERWAR"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ZGR
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

CARPAT_01_LEMKO = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = SCZ
			original_tag = LEM
			original_tag = GUR
			original_tag = BSK
		}
	}

	targets = {
		LEM
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
			NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		}
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SCZ
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.02.14
		LEM = { exists = yes }			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = LEM
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.02.14
		SCZ = { exists = yes }			
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = GUR
					original_tag = LEM
					original_tag = BSK
				}
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2029.02.11
		LEM = { exists = yes }	
		LEM = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }		
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision GAL_01_SALT_HYPERWAR"
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { original_tag = LEM }}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = LEM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { original_tag = LEM
			SCZ = { exists = yes }	
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SCZ
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}		
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

CARPAT_03_FINISH_HIM = {
	allowed = {
		is_tatry_region = yes
		NOT = {
			original_tag = BBA
			original_tag = WYM
		}
	}
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	visible = {
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 7
			LEM = { exists = no }
			SCZ = { exists = no }
			TYM = { exists = no }
			ZGR = { exists = no }
			GUR = { exists = no }
			ZKP = { exists = no }
			CIE = { exists = no }
			BSK = { exists = no }
		}
		OR = {
			BBA = {exists = yes}
			WYM = {exists = yes}
		}		
	}

	targets = {
		BBA
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	days_remove = 14
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1000
	}
	remove_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BBA
				BBA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		annex_country = {
			target = BBA
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BBA
				BBA = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BBA
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = WYM
				WYM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		annex_country = {
			target = WYM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = WYM
				WYM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WYM
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}				
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

#ZAGŁĘBIE I JURA - FAZA PIERWSZA


 ZAGJUR_01_JWK = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JUR
			original_tag = CCH
		}		
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JUR
			original_tag = CCH
		}
		OR = {
			JUR = { exists = no }
			CCH = { exists = no }
		}			
		NOT = { 
			has_idea = cooldown
		}
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = JWK } }
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.02.14
		CCH = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = CCH_intercounty }}
		JUR = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = JUR_intercounty }}
	}

	targets = {
		JWK
	}
	
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			original_tag = JWK
		}
	}	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = JWK
	complete_effect = {
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 15
		}
	}
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision ZAGJUR_01_JWK"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = JWK }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = JWK
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
 	}
 }

			}

				type = voivodeship_war
			}

			}
			}

		}
 	}

#██╔══██║██║░░██║██║░░░░░░░╚██╔╝░░  ██║░░██╗██╔══██╗██║░░██║░╚═══██╗░╚═══██╗
#██║░░██║╚█████╔╝███████╗░░░██║░░░  ╚█████╔╝██║░░██║╚█████╔╝██████╔╝██████╔╝
#╚═╝░░╚═╝░╚════╝░╚══════╝░░░╚═╝░░░  ░╚════╝░╚═╝░░╚═╝░╚════╝░╚═════╝░╚═════╝░
#ŚWIĘTOKRZYSKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 HOLY_CROSS_01_ROUND_ONE = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = NSZ
			original_tag = STO
			original_tag = NRA
			original_tag = STA
			original_tag = SND					
			original_tag = KEL				
		}
	}

	available = {
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { is_holy_cross = yes } }
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.06.01
		date < 2029.02.18
		NOT = {
			any_other_country = {
				has_country_flag = holy_cross_round_one
			}
			has_country_flag = holy_cross_round_one_fought
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100		
	}
	days_re_enable = 5
	days_remove = 3
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = holy_cross_round_one 
			set_country_flag = holy_cross_round_one_fought
		}
	}

	targets = {
		HOL
	}
	target_non_existing = yes

	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision holy_cross_round_one - fight"
		random_neighbor_country = { 
			limit = { 
				is_holy_cross = yes
				NOT = { original_tag = KIE }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			clr_country_flag = holy_cross_round_one 
		}
	}

	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		any_other_country = {
			has_country_flag = holy_cross_round_one
		}
	}
 }

#ŚWIĘTOKRZYSKIE - FAZA DRUGA

 HOLY_CROSS_01_ROUND_TWO = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = NSZ
			original_tag = STO
			original_tag = NRA
			original_tag = STA
			original_tag = SND					
			original_tag = KIE			
		}
	}

	available = {
		NOT = {
			any_other_country = {
				has_country_flag = holy_cross_round_two
			}
		}
		ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { is_holy_cross = yes } }
		has_war = no
		date > 2029.02.18
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100		
	}

	targets = {
		HOL
	}
	target_non_existing = yes

	days_remove = 14
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = holy_cross_round_two 
		}
	}
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision holy_cross_round_two - fight"
		random_neighbor_country = { 
			limit = { 
				is_holy_cross = yes
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			clr_country_flag = holy_cross_round_two 
		}
	}

	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		any_other_country = {
			has_country_flag = holy_cross_round_two
		}
	}
 }

LBL_01_MAFIA = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_lubelskie = yes
		is_lubelskie_tribe = no
	}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					original_tag = TEN
				}
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2027.05.04
		RMF = { exists = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { original_tag = TEN }
				}
			}
		has_war = no
		date > 2030.01.01
		TEN = { exists = no }
		RMF = { exists = yes }
		ROOT = { is_neighbor_of = RMF }
		}
	}

	targets = { RMF }
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			original_tag = RMF
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision LBL_01_RPP"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RMF
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

LBL_02_LUBLIN_WAR = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_lubelskie = yes
		is_lubelskie_tribe = no
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = CRN
			original_tag = KSN
			original_tag = SWD
		}
		has_war = no
		date > 2029.07.01
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision LBL_01_EAST_LUBLIN"
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = KSN } }
				KSN = {exists = yes}
			}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = KSN 
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SWD } }
				SWD = {exists = yes}
			}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SWD 
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CRN } }
				CRN = {exists = yes}
			}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CRN 
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}		
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

		}

#RADOMSKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA
 RADOM_03_RADOM_WAR = {
	
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_radom_province = yes
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2029.05.01
		RAD = { has_country_flag = radom_committed }
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision wojna na radomszczyznie"
		if = { limit = { country_exists = AIR
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = AIR 
						 is_in_faction_with = AIR } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = AIR
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = PAB
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = PAB 
						 is_in_faction_with = PAB } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = PAB
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SKA
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SKA
						 is_in_faction_with = SKA } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SKA
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = CZA
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CZA 
						 is_in_faction_with = CZA } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CZA
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SAT
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SAT 
						 is_in_faction_with = SAT } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SAT
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SZY
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SZY 
						 is_in_faction_with = SZY } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SZY
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
		if = { limit = { country_exists = APC
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = APC
						 is_in_faction_with = APC } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = APC
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}	
		if = { limit = { country_exists = GRJ
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = GRJ
						 is_in_faction_with = GRJ
						GRJ = { is_subject = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GRJ
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}	
		if = { limit = { country_exists = VRC
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = VRC
						 is_in_faction_with = VRC
						VRC = { is_subject = yes } } } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = VRC
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

#ŁÓDZKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 cleanup_lodzig_wars = { 
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = BBW
			original_tag = KRS
			original_tag = SAP
			original_tag = WML
			original_tag = ZHP
			original_tag = ZYD
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.03.01
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			original_tag = BBW
			original_tag = KRS
			original_tag = SAP
			AND = {
				original_tag = WML
				NOT = {
				country_exists = BBW
				country_exists = KRS
				country_exists = SAP
				country_exists = ZHP
				country_exists = ZYD
				}
			}
			original_tag = ZHP
			original_tag = ZYD
		}
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
		}
		ROOT = { NOT = { has_idea = cooldown } }
	}

	targets = {
		KAR TIG AMW RDM LKS RUT POG
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
			NOT = { is_subject = yes }
			NOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
		}			
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	complete_effect = {
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = {
			idea = cooldown
			days = 9
		}
	 }
	}
	days_remove = 7
	remove_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}

	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}

 }

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_capital_district = yes
			OR = {
				original_tag = TVP
				original_tag = TVN
			}
		}

	available = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TVP
				original_tag = TVN
			}
			has_war = no
			date > 2028.04.11 #Nie wiem kiedy dobrze by było zacząć, więc roboczo jest tutaj
			is_in_faction = no
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision WARSZAWA_TV_HYPERWAR"
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = TVP }
					country_exists = TVN 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TVN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = TVN }
					country_exists = TVP 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TVP
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

WARSZAWA_jaki_vs_mafia = { #wrc vs wol

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = WRC
			original_tag = WOL
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2031.07.15 #placeholder
		has_global_flag = warszawa_prawica_win
	}


	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	targets = {
		WRC WOL
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
			original_tag = WRC
			original_tag = WOL
			}
			NOT = { original_tag = ROOT }
		}			
	}

	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision WARSZAWA_jaki_vs_mafia"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

		OR = {
			original_tag = 	WAT
			original_tag = IPN
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2031.07.15 #placeholder
		has_global_flag = warszawa_prawica_win
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	targets = {
		WAT IPN
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
			original_tag = WAT
			original_tag = IPN
			}
			NOT = { original_tag = ROOT }
		}			
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision WARSZAWA_watvsipn"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

WARSZAWA_napierdalanka_o_centrum = { #KCZ/PLC VS IPN/WAT

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = WAT
			original_tag = IPN
			original_tag = KCZ
			original_tag = PLC
		}
		}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		date > 2031.07.15 #placeholder
		has_global_flag = warszawa_prawica_win
	}
	
	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision WARSZAWA_watvsipn"
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = WAT }
					country_exists = KCZ 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KCZ
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = WAT }
					country_exists = PLC 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PLC
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = IPN }
					country_exists = KCZ 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KCZ
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = IPN }
					country_exists = PLC 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PLC
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = KCZ }
					country_exists = IPN 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = IPN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { original_tag = KCZ }
					country_exists = WAT 
					}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WAT
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
}

	podlasie_plemiona = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		
		allowed = {
			is_podlasie = yes
			NOT = {
				is_podlasie_tribe = yes
				original_tag = AGR
				original_tag = SDL
			}
		}
		
		target_array = global.podlasie_tribes
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_podlasie_tribe = yes
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = BOM
						original_tag = KON
						original_tag = TAT
						original_tag = BEL
						original_tag = SAN
						original_tag = LMZ
					}
					ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { is_podlasie_tribe = yes } }
					FROM = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }
					FROM = { exists = yes }
					date > 2027.10.01
					has_war = no
					NOT = { has_idea = cooldown }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = SDL
						original_tag = AGR
						}
					ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { is_podlasie_tribe = yes } }
					FROM = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }
					FROM = { exists = yes }	
					count_triggers = {
							amount = 7
							TAT = {exists = no}
							SAN = {exists = no}
							LMZ = {exists = no}
							BEL = {exists = no}
							BOM = {exists = no}
							KON = {exists = no}
							SDL = {exists = no}
							AGR = {exists = no}
					}
					has_war = no
					NOT = { has_idea = cooldown }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		days_remove = 10
		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = cooldown
				days = 11
			}
		}
		remove_effect  = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [ROOT.GetName] fires decision podlasie_plemiona"
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = FROM
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
		}

 north_mazovia_war = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = POL
				original_tag = ORL
				original_tag = SAS
				original_tag = MAR
			}
		}

		available = {
			date > 2029.04.01
			has_war = no
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		days_remove = 4
		remove_effect  = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: Decision north_mazovia_war"
				if = { limit = { country_exists = ORL
								NOT = { has_war_with = ORL }
								 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ORL } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ORL
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = POL
							NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = POL } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = POL
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = SAS
							NOT = { has_war_with = SAS }
								 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SAS } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SAS
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = KUR 
						NOT = { has_war_with = KUR }
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = KUR } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KUR
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = ZWK
							NOT = { has_war_with = ZWK } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZWK } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ZWK
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = MAR
							NOT = { has_war_with = MAR } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MAR } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = MAR
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = PLO
							NOT = { has_war_with = PLO } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = PLO } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PLO
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = GOS
							NOT = { has_war_with = GOS } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = GOS } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GOS
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = SRP
							NOT = { has_war_with = SRP } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SRP } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SRP
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
				if = { limit = { country_exists = SCH
							NOT = { has_war_with = SCH } 
						 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = SCH } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SCH
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}				
		}

 russian_invasion = {
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	allowed = {
		original_tag = ROS
	}
	available = {
		ROS = { num_of_controlled_states > 1 
			has_government = autocracy
		}
		has_war = no
		date > 2028.02.19
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 5
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision russian_invasion"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = TEU
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = TEU } } }

				target = TEU

 anti_russian_front_decision = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = WRM 
	}

	available = {
		OR = {				
			date > 2028.04.01
			has_war_with = ROS
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 5
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision anti_russian_front"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ROS
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { original_tag = ROS }
				}
				ROOT = { 
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROS }
				}
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: Deccing on [ROS.GetName]"
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [WRM.GetName] creates Anti-Russian Front"
		create_faction_from_template = faction_template_regional
		set_faction_name = anti_russian_front
		log = "[GetDateText]: [WRM.GetName] adds [TEU.GetName] to Anti-Russian Front"
		add_to_faction = TEU
		log = "[GetDateText]: [WRM.GetName] adds [PZW.GetName] to Anti-Russian Front"
		add_to_faction = PZW
		log = "[GetDateText]: [WRM.GetName] adds [MRG.GetName] to Anti-Russian Front"
		add_to_faction = MRG
		log = "[GetDateText]: [WRM.GetName] adds [ELB.GetName] to Anti-Russian Front"
		add_to_faction = ELB
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			news_event = { 
				id = rosja.3
			}
		}
	}
 }

		TEU = { leave_faction = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [TEU.GetName] quits faction"
		ELB = { leave_faction = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [ELB.GetName] quits faction"
		MRG = { leave_faction = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [MRG.GetName] quits faction"
		WRM = { dismantle_faction = yes }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [WRM.GetName] dismantles faction"
		ROS = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = TEU
			}
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = LUB
			}
		}	
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_warmia_and_masuria_state = yes
				}
			}
			teleport_armies = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = TEU
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ROS = {
		random_list = {
				1 = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {  is_ai = no  }
						news_event = { 
							id = rosja.4
							days = 9
						}
					}
				}
				1 = {

#POMORSKIE - FAZA PIERWSZA
 POMGDA_gdansk_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = GDA
		#OR = {
		#	original_tag = GDA
		#	original_tag = MPR
		#	original_tag = BOL
		#}
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.03.05
		country_exists = GDA
		country_exists = MPR
		country_exists = BOL
		has_war = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	targets = {
		MPR BOL
	}

	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
			original_tag = MPR
			original_tag = BOL
			}
		}			
	}

	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}

	days_remove = 14

	war_with_target_on_complete = yes

	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision POMGDA_gdansk_war"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war_with = BOL
			has_war_with = MPR
		}
	}
 }

#POMORSKIE - FAZA DRUGA
 POMGDA_borowiacy_kociewie_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = CZL
			original_tag = LOT
		}
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.09.01
		country_exists = CZL
		country_exists = LOT
		has_war = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}

	days_remove = 14

	war_with_target_on_complete = yes

	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision POMGDA_borowiacy_kociewie_war"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CZL
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LOT
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = LTS
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = LTS
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = LOT
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CZL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CHG
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = CHG
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

 POMGDA_helows_kaszuby_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = HEL
			original_tag = OWS
			original_tag = KSZ
			original_tag = KSC
		}
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.09.01
		has_war = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}

	days_remove = 14

	war_with_target_on_complete = yes

	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision POMGDA_helows_kaszuby_war"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = HEL
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = KSZ
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KSZ
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = KSC
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KSC
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = OWS
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = KSZ
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KSZ
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = KSC
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KSC
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = KSZ
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = OWS
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = OWS
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = HEL
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = HEL
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = KSC
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = OWS
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = OWS
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = HEL
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = HEL
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

#POMORSKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA
 POMGDA_pomorze_jednoczenie_war = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_pomerelia = yes
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 8
				HEL = { exists = no }
				OWS = { exists = no }
				GAY = { exists = no }
				RLE = { exists = no }
				KSZ = { exists = no }
				KSC = { exists = no }	
				GDA = { exists = no }
				BOL = { exists = no }
				MPR = { exists = no }
				KOR = { exists = no }
				CZL = { exists = no }
				LOT = { exists = no }	
			}
			date > 2029.06.01
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = unified_voivodeship 
			#has_country_flag = getting_ready_to_war_pomerelia
			OR = {
				original_tag = GDY
				original_tag = ARK
			}
			has_idea = war_declaration_cooldown
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	##fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}

	days_remove = 14
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes

	target_array = root.neighbors
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_pomerelia = yes
		}
	}

	complete_effect = {
		#set_country_flag = getting_ready_to_war_pomerelia
		log = "[GetDateText]: [ROOT.GetName] is getting ready to war in Pomorze..."
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = war_declaration_cooldown
			days = 20
		}
	}
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision POMGDA_pomorze_jednoczenie_war"
		#clr_country_flag = getting_ready_to_war_pomerelia
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	#cancel_trigger = {
	#	ROOT = {
	#		has_war = yes
	#	}
	#}
 }

			}			
		}

		available = {

			has_war = no
			date > 2028.03.03
		}

		targets = {
			FRE
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				original_tag = FRE
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {

		}
		#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
		days_remove = 14
		war_with_on_remove = FRE

					target = FRE
					type = voivodeship_war
				}
				}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {

			}

		}

			OR = {
				ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = USP } }
				ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = JAS } }
				ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = NOR } }
			}
			#ROOT = { any_neighbor_country = { original_tag = EKW } }

					limit = { 
							country_exists = NOR
							ROOT = { original_tag = USP }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = NOR
						type = voivodeship_war
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
							country_exists = NOR
							ROOT = { original_tag = JAS }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = NOR
						type = voivodeship_war
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
							country_exists = USP
							NOT = { country_exists = JAS }
							ROOT = { original_tag = NOR }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = USP
						type = voivodeship_war
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
							country_exists = JAS
							NOT = { country_exists = USP }
							ROOT = { original_tag = NOR }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = JAS
						type = voivodeship_war
					}
				}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
 		}

					limit = { 
						is_neighbor_of = SWI
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = SWI
						type = voivodeship_war
					}

						ROOT = { original_tag = NOR }

						}
					}

#KALISKIE - FAZA OSTATECZNA
 barbarian_raid = {
	allowed = {
		always = yes
	}
	visible = {
		has_idea = barbarians_idea
		CAL = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = CAL_empire_or_death
				has_completed_focus = CAL_adapt_or_perish
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = CAL_barbarians_win_flag
		}
	}
	target_array = root.neighbors
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			# NOT = {
			# 	has_war = yes
			# }
			is_somsiad = no
			NOT = {
				original_tag = ZON
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				original_tag = WIZ
				original_tag = SAX
				original_tag = OST
				original_tag = JUT
				original_tag = FRK
				original_tag = HNN
				original_tag = SCY
				original_tag = AES
				original_tag = VAN
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = CAL
					original_tag = PRT
				}
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = CAL_empire_or_death
					OR = {
						ROOT = {
							original_tag = JUT
						}
						ROOT = {
							original_tag = HNN
						}
						ROOT = {
							original_tag = VAN
						}
						
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	war_with_target_on_complete = yes
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
	}

	remove_effect = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
 }

 LEGNICA_01_EKS_LOSU_LOSU = { #a wiecie co kurwa, polosujmy

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		original_tag = EKS
	}

	available = {
		date > 2028.04.01
		country_exists = ECO
		country_exists = BOG
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 14
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision EKS_annex_EKS_BOG"
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ECO
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = BOG
					transfer_troops = yes
				}				
			}
			20 = {
				ECO = {
					annex_country = {
						target = EKS
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = BOG
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			10 = {
				BOG = {
					annex_country = {
						target = EKS
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = ECO
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = BOG_eurokom
				}
			}
		}

	}
	
 }

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war

			original_tag = BOG
			original_tag = ECO
			original_tag = CYG
			original_tag = KGH
			original_tag = TOU
		}
	}

	available = {
		date > 2029.03.15
		has_war = no
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = EKS
			}
			OR = {
				TOU = { exists = no }
				TOU = { is_subject = yes }
			}
			OR = {
				KGH = {exists=yes}
				CYG = {exists=yes}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ECO
			}
			OR = {
				TOU = { exists = no }
				TOU = { is_subject = yes }
			}
			OR = {
				KGH = {exists=yes}
				CYG = {exists=yes}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = BOG
			}
			OR = {
				TOU = { exists = no }
				TOU = { is_subject = yes }
			}
			OR = {
				KGH = {exists=yes}
				CYG = {exists=yes}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = KGH
			}
			OR = {
				TOU = { exists = no }
				TOU = { is_subject = yes }
			}
			OR = {
				EKS = {exists=yes}
				ECO = {exists=yes}
				BOG = {exists=yes}
			}
			CYG = { exists = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CYG
			}
			OR = {
				TOU = { exists = no }
				TOU = { is_subject = yes }
			}
			OR = {
				EKS = {exists=yes}
				ECO = {exists=yes}
				BOG = {exists=yes}
			}
			KGH = { exists = no }
		}								
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = KGH
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision EKS_KGH_war"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = TOU
				TOU = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = TOU }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TOU
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ECO
				ECO = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ECO }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ECO
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = EKS
				EKS = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = EKS }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = EKS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BOG
				BOG = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = BOG }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BOG
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = KGH
				KGH = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = KGH }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KGH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CYG
				CYG = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CYG }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CYG
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}		
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}

		}

			limit = {
				country_exists = WIN
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = WIN }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WIN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PZL
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = PZL }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PZL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ZAG
				ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZAG }}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ZAG
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
		}				
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

WROC_01_OLE_OLE = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_lower_silesia = yes 
		NOT = {
			original_tag = OLE
		}
	}

	available = {
		OLE = { exists = yes }
		OLE = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 2027.11.01
				original_tag = RYB
			}
			AND = {
				date > 2029.01.01
				OR = {
					AND = {
					original_tag = MPK
					NOT = { is_subject_of = WRO }
					}
					original_tag = WRO
				}
			}
			AND = {
				date > 2031.01.01
				OR = {
					original_tag = ANA
					original_tag = MNL
					original_tag = ZUL
					original_tag = CZE
				}
			}			
		}
		has_war = no
	}
	targets = {
		OLE
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			original_tag = OLE
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	days_remove = 14
	war_with_on_remove = OLE
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision RYB_OLE_war"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = OLE
			type = voivodeship_war
		}
	}
	cancel_trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
 }

 WROC_03_MARCH_SOUTH = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = WRO
			original_tag = RYB
			original_tag = MPK
		}		
	}

	available = {
		has_war = no
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = WRO
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					WRO = { NOT = { has_country_flag = WRO_makao} }
					OR = {
						MPK = {exists = no}
						MPK = {is_subject_of = WRO}
					}
					RYB = {exists=no}
				}
				AND = {
					WRO = { has_country_flag = WRO_makao }
					OR = {
						ZUL = { exists = yes}
						ANA = { exists = yes}
						MNL = { exists = yes}
						CZE = { exists = yes}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = MPK
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					WRO = { exists = no }
					RYB = { exists = no }
				}
				AND = {
					WRO = { has_country_flag = WRO_makao }
					RYB = { exists = no }
					MPK = {
						NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = {
								modifier = dam_blown_modifier
							}
						}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = RYB
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					WRO = { exists = no }
					MPK = { exists = no }
				}
				AND = {
					WRO = { has_country_flag = WRO_makao }
					MPK = { exists = no }
				}
			}
		}				
	}

		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 20
	remove_effect  = {

		ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MNL }}
			} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MNL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = WRO 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = WRO }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WRO
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = MPK 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MPK }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MPK
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}			
			if = { limit = { country_exists = CZE 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = CZE }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CZE
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = RYB 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = RYB }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RYB
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = ZUL 
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ZUL }}
		} 
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ZUL
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = ANA
			ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = ANA }}

 battle_of_nysa = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_opolskie = yes
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = NYS
			original_tag = LEH
			OR = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = LCH
					OPO = { exists = no }
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = OPO
					LCH = { exists = no }
				}				
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = OPOLE_BORDER_WAR_END
		date > 2028.06.27
	}

	

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100

	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	visible = {
		has_war = no
	}
	days_remove = 11
	remove_effect  = {	
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision opole_battle_of_nysa"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = NYS
							NOT = { has_war_with = NYS}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = NYS } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = NYS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = LEH 
			NOT = { has_war_with = LEH}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = LEH } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LEH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
 		}
 }

 opole_gotterdammerung = {

	icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
	
	allowed = {
		is_opolskie = yes
	}

	available = {
		has_global_flag = OPOLE_BORDER_WAR_END
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 2029.06.01
				has_war = no
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					OPO = { exists = no }
					MNI = { exists = no }
					LCH = { exists = no }
					LEH = { exists = no }
					WND = { exists = no }
					NYS = { exists = no }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				date > 2030.08.01
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					OPO = { exists = no }
					MNI = { exists = no }
					LCH = { exists = no }
					LEH = { exists = no }
					WND = { exists = no }
					NYS = { exists = no }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

	days_remove = 14
	days_re_enable = 30
	remove_effect  = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: Decision opole_gotterdammerung"
			if = { limit = { country_exists = NYS
							NOT = { has_war_with = NYS}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = NYS } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = NYS
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = LEH 
			NOT = { has_war_with = LEH}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = LEH } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LEH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = LCH
							NOT = { has_war_with = LCH}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = LCH } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LCH
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = OPO 
			NOT = { has_war_with = OPO}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = OPO } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = OPO
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = WAN
							NOT = { has_war_with = WAN}
							 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = WAN } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WAN
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
			if = { limit = { country_exists = MNI 
			NOT = { has_war_with = MNI}
					 ROOT = { NOT = { original_tag = MNI } } }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MNI
				type = voivodeship_war
			}
			}
	}

 		cancel_trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
 		}
 }


}
